16/11/21, 11:01â€¯pm - @Hemant Soni: #include <stdio.h>
#include<stdlib.h>
#define Max 10
int top = -1;
int stack[Max];
void push(){
  if(top == Max-1){
    printf("Overflow condition \n\n");
  }else{
    top++;
    scanf("%d",&stack[top]);
    
  }
}
void pop(){
  if(top == -1){
    printf("Underflow condition \n\n");
  }else{
  printf("%d is deleted \n",stack[top]);
  top --;
  }
}
void display(){
  if(top == -1){
    printf("Stack is empty \n\n");
  }else{
    int i;
    for(i=0;i<=top;i++)
    printf("%d\n",stack[i]);
  }
}
int exit1(){
  printf("You are exited");
  return 1;
}
int main()
{
  int a=0,n;
  while(1){
    printf("1 Push\n");
    printf("2 Pop\n");
    printf("3 Display\n");
    printf("4 exit\n");
    printf("Enter your choice:-");
    scanf("%d",&n);
    switch(n){
      case 1:push();
      break;
      case 2:pop();
      break;
      case 3:display();
      break;
      case 4:a=exit1();
      break;
      default:printf("Invalid input \n");
    }
    if(a==1)
    break;
  }
  return 0;
}

16/11/21, 11:01â€¯pm - @Hemant Soni: #include<stdio.h>
#define MAX 100
int rear=-1;
int front=-1;
int Queue[MAX];

void enqueue(){
    int element;
    printf("Enter Element :- \n");
    scanf("%d",&element);
    if(rear==MAX-1){
        printf("OverFlow Condition");
    }
    else{
        if(front==-1&&rear==-1){
            front=0;
            rear=0;
        }
        else{
            rear=rear+1;
        }
        Queue[rear]=element;
    }
}

void dequeue(){
    if(front==rear){
        printf("UnderFlow Comdition");
    }
    else{
        int temp=Queue[front];
        front++;
        printf("Item was Succefully Deleted");
    }
}

void print(){
    if(front==rear){
        printf("Stack Was Empty");
    }
    else{
        int i;
        for(i=front;i<=rear;i++){
            printf("%d \n",Queue[i]);
        }
    }
}

int main(){
    int choice;
    while (1)
    {
        printf("1.Press 1 for inserting Element\n");
        printf("2.Press 2 for Deleting Element\n");
        printf("3.Press 3 for Printing All Element\n");
        printf("4.Press 4 for Exit\n");
        scanf("%d",&choice);
        switch (choice)
        {
        case 1:enqueue();
            break;
        case 2:dequeue();
        break;
        case 3:print();
        break;
        case 4:exit(1);
        break;
        default:
        printf("Invalid Operation");
            break;
        }

    }
    
}

14/12/21, 12:19â€¯pm - @Hemant Soni: #include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
struct node
{
    int data;
    struct node *addrs;
};

struct node *head = NULL;
struct node *temp1, *temp2, *temp3, *temp4, *temp5, *temp6;
struct node *newno;

void insertSTll()
{
    if (head == NULL)
    {
        newno = (struct node *)malloc(sizeof(struct node));
        printf("Enter value / info of the node :- ");
        scanf("%d", &newno->data);
        newno->addrs = NULL;
        head = newno;
    }
    else
    {
        temp4 = head;
        newno = (struct node *)malloc(sizeof(struct node));
        printf("Enter value / info of the node :- ");
        scanf("%d", &newno->data);
        newno->addrs = temp4;
        head = newno;
    }
}

void insertLAll()
{
    if (head == NULL)
    {
        newno = (struct node *)malloc(sizeof(struct node));
        printf("Enter value / info of the node :- ");
        scanf("%d", &newno->data);
        newno->addrs = NULL;
        head = newno;
        temp1 = newno;
    }
    else
    {
    	temp1 = head;
    	while(1){
    		if(temp1->addrs !=NULL)
    		    temp1 = temp1->addrs;
    		else
    		    break;
		}
		
        newno = ((struct node *)malloc(sizeof(struct node)));
        printf("Enter value / info of the node :- ");
        scanf("%d", &newno->data);
        newno->addrs = head->addrs;
        temp1->addrs = newno;
        temp1 = newno;
    }
}

void insertASll()
{
    int n;
    printf("\nEnter data / value / info of node after that insertion takes place :- ");
    scanf("%d", &n);

    temp5 = head;
    while (1)
    {

        if (temp5->data == n)
        {
            newno = ((struct node *)malloc(sizeof(struct node)));
            printf("Enter value / info of the node :- ");
            scanf("%d", &newno->data);
            newno->addrs = temp5->addrs;
            temp5->addrs = newno;
            break;
        }
        else if (temp5->addrs == NULL)
        {
            printf("Given Data is not match with the linklist \n");
            break;
        }
        else
        {
            temp5 = temp5->addrs;
        }
    }
}

void deletionSTll()
{
    if (head == NULL)
    {
        printf("\n\nUnderflow!!!\n\n");
    }
    else
    {
        printf("\n%d is deleted\n", head->data);
        head = head->addrs;
    }
}

void deletionLAll()
{
    if (head == NULL)
    {
        printf("\n\nUnderflow!!!\n\n");
    }
    else
    {
        temp3 = head;
        while (temp3->addrs->addrs != NULL)
        {
            temp3 = temp3->addrs;
        }
        printf("\n%d is deleted\n", temp3->addrs->data);
        temp3->addrs = NULL;
    }
}

void deletionASll()
{
    if (head == NULL)
    {
        printf("\n\nUnderflow!!!\n\n");
    }
    else
    {
        int n, a;
        printf("\nEnter data / value / info of node after that deletion takes place :- ");
        scanf("%d", &n);
        temp6 = head;
        while (a < 1)
        {
            if (temp6->addrs == NULL)
            {
                printf("Given Data is not match with the linklist ");
            }
            else if (temp6->addrs->data == n)
            {
                a++;
            }
            else
            {
                temp6 = temp6->addrs;
            }
        }
        printf("\n%d is deleted\n", temp6->addrs->data);
        temp6->addrs = temp6->addrs->addrs;
    }
}

void displayll()
{
    if (head == NULL)
    {
        printf("\n\nList is Empty!!!\n");
    }
    else
    {
        printf("\n");
        temp2 = head;
        while (1)         
        {
            printf(" %d ", temp2->data);
            temp2 = temp2->addrs;
            if (temp2 != head)
            {
                printf("->");
            }
            if(temp2 == head){
              break;
            }
        }
        printf("\n");
    }
}

int main()
{
    int n, a = 0;
    while (a<1)
    {
        printf("\n1. Insert in linklist at start \n");
        printf("2. Insert in linklist at last \n");
        printf("3. Insert in linklist at a certain position \n");
        printf("4. Delete from starting  \n");
        printf("5. Delete from last  \n");
        printf("6. Delete from a certain position  \n");
        printf("7. Display  \n");
        printf("8. Search a value  \n");
        printf("9. Exit from linklist \n");
        printf("Enter your choice :- ");
        scanf("%d", &n);
        switch (n)
        {
        case 1:
            insertSTll();
            break;

        case 2:
            insertLAll();
            break;

        case 3:
            insertASll();
            break;

        case 4:
            deletionSTll();
            break;

        case 5:
            deletionLAll();
            break;

        case 6:
            deletionASll();
            break;

        case 7:
            displayll();
            break;

        default:
            a = a + 1;
            free(temp1);
            free(temp2);
            free(head);
            free(newno);
            printf("\nYou are exited"); 
        }
    }
    return 0;
}

#include <stdlib.h>

struct node
{
    int data;
    struct node *left;
    struct node *right;
};

struct node *root = NULL;
struct node *newno;
struct node *temp1, *temp2, *temp3, *temp4;

void insertRo(int value)
{
    root = (struct node *)malloc(sizeof(struct node));
    root->data = value;
    root->left = NULL;
    root->right = NULL;
}

void insertLf(int value)
{
    if (root->left == NULL)
    {
        if (value <= root->data)
        {
            newno = (struct node *)malloc(sizeof(struct node));
            newno->data = value;
            newno->left = NULL;
            newno->right = NULL;
            root->left = newno;
            temp1 = newno;
            temp3 = temp1;
        }
    }
    else
    {
        temp1 = temp3;
        while (1)
        {
            if (temp1->data > value)
                if (temp1->left == NULL)
                    break;
                else
                    temp1 = temp1->left;

            else if (temp1->right == NULL)
                break;
            else
                temp1 = temp1->right;
        }
        if (value < temp1->data)
        {
            newno = (struct node *)malloc(sizeof(struct node));
            newno->data = value;
            newno->left = NULL;
            newno->right = NULL;
            temp1->left = newno;
        }
        else
        {
            newno = (struct node *)malloc(sizeof(struct node));
            newno->data = value;
            newno->left = NULL;
            newno->right = NULL;
            temp1->right = newno;
        }
    }
}

void insertRt(int value)
{
    if (root->right == NULL)
    {
        if (value > root->data)
        {
            newno = (struct node *)malloc(sizeof(struct node));
            newno->data = value;
            newno->left = NULL;
            newno->right = NULL;
            root->right = newno;
            temp2 = newno;
            temp4 = temp2;
        }
    }
    else
    {
        temp2 = temp4;
        while (1)
        {
            if (temp2->data > value)
                if (temp2->left == NULL)
                    break;
                else
                    temp2 = temp2->left;

            else if (temp2->right == NULL)
                break;
            else
                temp2 = temp2->right;
        }
        if (value < temp2->data)
        {
            newno = (struct node *)malloc(sizeof(struct node));
            newno->data = value;
            newno->left = NULL;
            newno->right = NULL;
            temp2->left = newno;
            temp2 = newno;
        }
        else
        {
            newno = (struct node *)malloc(sizeof(struct node));
            newno->data = value;
            newno->left = NULL;
            newno->right = NULL;
            temp2->right = newno;
            temp2 = newno;
        }
    }
}

void inordertraversal(struct node *temp5)
{
    if (temp5 == NULL)
        return;
    inordertraversal(temp5->left);
    printf("%4d", temp5->data);
    inordertraversal(temp5->right);
}

void preodertraversal(struct node *temp6)
{
    if (temp6 == NULL)
        return;
    printf("%4d", temp6->data);
    preodertraversal(temp6->left);
    preodertraversal(temp6->right);
}

void postordertraversal(struct node *temp7)
{
    if (temp7 == NULL)
        return;
    postordertraversal(temp7->left);
    postordertraversal(temp7->right);
    printf("%4d", temp7->data);
}

int main()
{
    int n, a = 0, value;
    for (; a < 1;)
    {
        printf("\n1. Insert \n");
        printf("2. Display tree Inorder \n");
        printf("3. Display tree Preorder \n");
        printf("4. Display tree Postorder \n");
        printf("5. Exit from queue \n");
        printf("Enter your choice :- ");
        scanf("%d", &n);
        switch (n)
        {
        case 1:
            printf("Enter data / value :- ");
            scanf("%d", &value);
            if (root == NULL)
                insertRo(value);
            else if (value < root->data)
                insertLf(value);
            else
                insertRt(value);
            break;

        case 2:
            inordertraversal(root);
            break;

        case 3:
            preodertraversal(root);
            break;

        case 4:
            postordertraversal(root);
            break;

        default:
            a = 1;
        }
    }
    printf("\nYou are exited !!\n");
    return 0;
}

using namespace std;

struct TreeNode
{
    int info;
    TreeNode* left;
    TreeNode* right;
};

//create new node
TreeNode* GetNewNode(int info)
{
    TreeNode* NewNode=new TreeNode();
    NewNode->info=info;
    NewNode->left=NewNode->right=NULL;
    return NewNode;
}

//insert new node
TreeNode* insert(TreeNode* root,int info)
{
    if(root==NULL)
    {
        return GetNewNode(info);
    }
    else if(info<=root->info)
    {
        root->left=insert(root->left,info);
    }
    else
    {
        root->right=insert(root->right,info);
    }
    return root;
}

void inorder(struct TreeNode *root) {
   if (root != NULL) {
      inorder(root->left);
      cout<<root->info<<" ";
      inorder(root->right);
   }
}
int main()
{
    //empty tree
    TreeNode* root=NULL;
    //elements in tree
    cout<<"Enter number of elements"<<endl;
    int num,temp;
    cin>>num;
    //insertion of elements
    for(int i=0;i<num;i++)
   {
       cout<<"Enter the node:"<<endl;
       cin>>temp;
       insert(root,temp);
   }
   inorder(root);
   return 0;
}

    inorder(root->left);
    cout<<root->info<<" ";
    inorder(root->right);
   }
}

void preorder(struct TreeNode* root)
{
    if(root==NULL)
    {
        return;
    }
    else
    {
        cout<<root->info<<" ";
        preorder(root->left);
        preorder(root->right);
    }
}

void postorder(struct TreeNode* root)
{
    if(root==NULL)
    {
        return;
    }
    else
    {
        preorder(root->right);
        preorder(root->left);
        cout<<root->info<<" ";
    }
}

int main()
{
    //elements in tree
    cout<<"Enter number of elements"<<endl;
    int num,temp,ch;
    cin>>num;
    //insertion of elements
    for(int i=0;i<num;i++)
   {
       cout<<"Enter the node:"<<endl;
       cin>>temp;
       root=insert(root,temp);
   }
   cout<<"Choose traversal option:"<<endl;
   cout<<"1-Inorder\n2-Preorder\n3-Postorder"<<endl;
   cin>>ch;
   switch(ch)
   {
       case 1:inorder(root);
       break;
       case 2:preorder(root);
       break;
       case 3:postorder(root);
       break;
   }
   return 0;
}

17/06/22, 10:34â€¯pm - Kanishk Pratap Singh: vector<int> rotateLeft(int d, vector<int> arr) {
vector<int> temp;
for(int i=0;i<d;i++)
{
    temp.push_back(arr[0]);
    arr.erase(arr.begin());
    arr.push_back(temp[0]);
    temp.pop_back();
}
return arr;
}

28/09/22, 12:31â€¯pm - @Hemant Soni: #include <iostream>

using namespace std;

int partition(int A[], int lb, int ub)
{
    int pivot = A[lb];
    int i = lb + 1;
    int j = ub;
    do
    {
        while (A[i] <= pivot)
            i++;
        while (A[j] > pivot)
            j--;

        if (i < j)
            swap(A[i],A[j]);
    }while(i<j);
    swap(A[lb],A[j]);
    return j;
}

void quicksort(int a[], int low, int high)
{
    int PartitionIN;
    if (low < high)
    {
        PartitionIN = partition(a, low, high);
        quicksort(a, low, PartitionIN - 1);
        quicksort(a, PartitionIN + 1, high);
    }
}

int main()
{
    int n, i            ;
    cout<<"Enter number of elements for QuickSort :- ";
    cin>>n;

    int ar[n];
    cout<<"Enter the elements for QuickSort :- ";
    for (i = 0; i < n; i++)
        cin>>ar[i];
    cout<<"Given elements for sorting is :-  ";
    for (i = 0; i < n; i++)
        cout<<ar[i]<<"\t";
    quicksort(ar, 0, n - 1);
    cout<<"\nSorted array is :- ";
    for (i = 0; i < n; i++)
        cout<<ar<<"\t";
    return 0;
}

09/11/22, 12:16â€¯pm - @Hemant Soni: +

#include <iostream>
using namespace std;

// defining the number of vertices
#define nV 4

#define INF 999

void printMatrix(int matrix[][nV]);

// Implementing floyd warshall algorithm
void floydWarshall(int graph[][nV]) {
  int matrix[nV][nV], i, j, k;

  for (i = 0; i < nV; i++)
    for (j = 0; j < nV; j++)
      matrix[i][j] = graph[i][j];

  // Adding vertices individually
  for (k = 0; k < nV; k++) {
    for (i = 0; i < nV; i++) {
      for (j = 0; j < nV; j++) {
        if (matrix[i][k] + matrix[k][j] < matrix[i][j])
          matrix[i][j] = matrix[i][k] + matrix[k][j];
      }
    }
  }
  printMatrix(matrix);
}

void printMatrix(int matrix[][nV]) {
  for (int i = 0; i < nV; i++) {
    for (int j = 0; j < nV; j++) {
      if (matrix[i][j] == INF)
        printf("%4s", "INF");
      else
        printf("%4d", matrix[i][j]);
    }
    printf("\n");
  }
}

int main() {
  int graph[nV][nV] = {{0, 3, INF, 5},
             {2, 0, INF, 4},
             {INF, 1, 0, INF},
             {INF, INF, 2, 0}};
  floydWarshall(graph);
}

06/12/22, 9:44â€¯am - @Hemant Soni: #include <graphics.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <conio.h>
#include <math.h>
int main()
{
    int gm;
    int gd = DETECT;
    int x1, x2, x3, y1, y2, y3, nx1, nx2, nx3, ny1, ny2, ny3, c;
    int sx, sy, xt, yt, r;
    bool l = true;
    float t;
    initgraph(&gd, &gm, (char *)"");
    printf("Enter the points of triangle :- ");
    setcolor(15);
    scanf("%d%d%d%d%d%d", &x1, &y1, &x2, &y2, &x3, &y3);
   // line(x1, y1, x2, y2);
   // line(x2, y2, x3, y3);
   // line(x3, y3, x1, y1);
    int cone[8]={x1,y1,x2,y2,x3,y3,x1,y1};
    drawpoly(4,cone);
    printf("\n 1.Transaction\n 2.Rotation\n 3.Scalling\n 4.exit");
    printf("Enter your choice:");
    scanf("%d", &c);
    while (l)
    {
        printf("Enter your choice:");
        scanf("%d", &c);
        switch (c)
        {
        case 1:
            printf("\n Enter the translation factor");
            scanf("%d%d", &xt, &yt);
            nx1 = x1 + xt;
            ny1 = y1 + yt;
            nx2 = x2 + xt;
            ny2 = y2 + yt;
            nx3 = x3 + xt;
            ny3 = y3 + yt;
            //line(nx1, ny1, nx2, ny2);
            //line(nx2, ny2, nx3, ny3);
            //line(nx3, ny3, nx1, ny1);
            drawpoly(4,cone);
            break;

        case 2:
            printf("\n Enter the angle of rotation");
            scanf("%d", &r);
            t = 3.14 * r / 180;
            nx1 = abs(x1 * cos(t) - y1 * sin(t));
            ny1 = abs(x1 * sin(t) + y1 * cos(t));
            nx2 = abs(x2 * cos(t) - y2 * sin(t));
            ny2 = abs(x2 * sin(t) + y2 * cos(t));
            nx3 = abs(x3 * cos(t) - y3 * sin(t));
            ny3 = abs(x3 * sin(t) + y3 * cos(t));
            //line(nx1, ny1, nx2, ny2);
            //line(nx2, ny2, nx3, ny3);
            //line(nx3, ny3, nx1, ny1);
            drawpoly(4,cone);
            break;
        case 3:
            printf("\n Enter the scalling factor");
            scanf("%d%d", &sx, &sy);
            nx1 = x1 * sx;
            ny1 = y2 * sy;
            nx2 = x2 * sx;
            ny2 = y2 * sy;
            nx3 = x3 * sx;
            ny3 = y3 * sy;
            //line(nx1, ny1, nx2, ny2);
            //line(nx2, ny2, nx3, ny3);
            //line(nx3, ny3, nx1, ny1);
            drawpoly(4,cone);
            break;

        case 4:
            l = false;
            break;
        default:
            printf("Enter the correct choice");
        }
    }
    getch();
}

04/01/23, 10:23â€¯am - @Hemant Soni: #include<graphics.h>
#include<conio.h>
#include<stdio.h>
#include<math.h>
int main()
{
    int in_point[4]= {0,0,0,0},out_point[4]= {0,0,0,0},check[4];

    int flag=0;
    float slope;
    int x,y,x1,y1;
    int gd=DETECT,gm;
    initgraph(&gd,&gm,(char*)"");

    printf("Enter x1,y1,x2,y2 of line :- ");
    scanf("%d%d%d%d",&x,&y,&x1,&y1);

    int window[10]= {50,50,450,50,450,450,50,450,50,50};

    drawpoly(5,window);
    line(x,y,x1,y1);


    if(y>450)
    {
        in_point[0]=1;
        flag=1 ;
    }
    if(y<50)
    {
        in_point[1]=1;
        flag=1;
    }
    if(x>450)
    {
        in_point[2]=1;
        flag=1;
    }
    if(x<50)
    {
        in_point[3]=1;
        flag=1;
    }


    if(y1>450)
    {
        out_point[0]=1;
        flag=1;
    }
    if(y1<50)
    {
        out_point[1]=1;
        flag=1;
    }
    if(x1>450)
    {
        out_point[2]=1;
        flag=1;
    }
    if(x1<50)
    {
        out_point[3]=1;
        flag=1;
    }
    if(flag==0)
    {
        printf("\nLine is Inside !!!");
    }
    else
    {


        flag=1;
        for(int i=0; i<4; i++)
        {
            check[i]= in_point[i] && out_point[i] ;
            if(check[i]==1)
                flag=0;
        }
        if(flag==0)
        {
            printf("\nLine is outside !!!!!");
        }
        else
        {
            printf("\nLine is partial inside need for line clipping !!!!!");
            slope=(float)(y1-y)/(x1-x);
            if(in_point[2]==0 && in_point[3]==1)
            {
                y=y+(float) (50-x)*slope ;
                x=50;

            }
            if(in_point[2]==1 && in_point[3]==0)
            {
                y=y+(float) (450-x)*slope ;
                x=450;

            }
            if(in_point[0]==1 && in_point[1]==0)
            {
                x=x+(float) (450-y)/slope ;
                y=450;

            }
            if(in_point[0]==0 && in_point[1]==1)
            {
                x=x+(float) (50-y)/slope ;
                y=50;

            }
            if(out_point[2]==0 && out_point[3]==1)
            {
                y1=y1+(float) (50-x1)*slope ;
                x1=50;

            }
            if(out_point[2]==1 && out_point[3]==0)
            {
                y1=y1+(float) (450-x1)*slope ;
                x1=450;

            }
            if(out_point[0]==1 && out_point[1]==0)
            {
                x1=x1+(float) (450-y1)/slope ;
                y1=450;

            }
            if(out_point[0]==0 && out_point[1]==1)
            {
                x1=x1+(float) (50-y1)/slope ;
                y1=50;
            }

            printf("\nNew Line Coordinates are (%d,%d) -> (%d,%d) !!!!!",x,y,x1,y1);
            delay(3000);
            clearviewport();
            drawpoly(5,window);
            //setcolor(RED);
            line(x,y,x1,y1);
        }
    }

    getch();
    return 0;
}

14/01/23, 10:13â€¯pm - @Hemant Soni: #include<graphics.h>
#include<stdio.h>
#include<conio.h>
#include<math.h>
int gd,gm,i,c,c2;
double x1,x2;
//y1,
double y3;
double y2,x,y,z,t,temp,temp1;
void draw(double[20][3]);
int main()
{
    do
    {
        double edge[20][3]= { 100,0,0,
                              100,100,0,
                              0,100,0,
                              0,100,100,
                              0,0,100,
                              0,0,0,
                              100,0,0,
                              100,0,100,
                              100,100,100,
                              100,100,100,
                              100,100,100,
                              100,100,0,
                              100,100,100,
                              100,100,100,
                              100,100,100,
                              0,100,100,
                              0,100,0,
                              0,0,0,
                              0,0,100,
                              100,0,100
                            };
//        clrscr();
        printf("Choose any one 3D Transformation : ");
        printf("\n\t1. Translation ");
        printf("\n\t2. Rotation ");
        printf("\n\t3. Scaling ");
        printf("\nEnter your choice : \t");
        scanf("%d",&c);
        switch(c)
        {
        case 1:
            printf("\nEnter the translation factors(tx,ty,tz) : \t");
            scanf("%lf%lf%lf",&x,&y,&z);
            draw(edge);
            for(i=0; i<20; i++)
            {
                edge[i][0]+=x;
                edge[i][1]+=y;
                edge[i][2]+=z;
            }
            draw(edge);
            break;
        case 2:
            printf("\n\n\t1.Rotation about X Axis ");
            printf("\n\t2. Rotation about Y Axis ");
            printf("\n\t3. Rotation about Z Axis ");
            printf("\nEnter your choice : \t");
            scanf("%d",&c2);
            printf("\n\nEnter the angle of rotation : \t");
            scanf("%lf",&t);
            t=(t*3.14)/180;
            switch(c2)
            {
            case 1:
                draw(edge);
                for(i=0; i<20; i++)
                {
                    temp=edge[i][1];
                    temp1=edge[i][2];
                    edge[i][1]=temp*cos(t)-temp1*sin(t);
                    edge[i][2]=temp*sin(t)+temp1*cos(t);
                }
                draw(edge);
                break;
            case 2:
                draw(edge);
                for(i=0; i<20; i++)
                {
                    temp=edge[i][0];
                    temp1=edge[i][2];
                    edge[i][0]=temp*cos(t)+temp1*sin(t);
                    edge[i][2]=-temp*sin(t)+temp1*cos(t);
                }
                draw(edge);
                break;
            case 3:
                draw(edge);
                for(i=0; i<20; i++)
                {
                    temp=edge[i][0];
                    temp1=edge[i][1];
                    edge[i][0]=temp*cos(t)-temp1*sin(t);
                    edge[i][1]=temp*sin(t)+temp1*cos(t);
                }
                draw(edge);
                break;
            }
            break;
        case 3:
            printf("\n\nEnter the scaling factors (sx,sy,sz) : \t");
            scanf("%lf%lf%lf",&x,&y,&z);
            draw(edge);
            for(i=0; i<20; i++)
            {
                edge[i][0]*=x;
                edge[i][1]*=y;
                edge[i][2]*=z;
            }
            draw(edge);
            break;
        }
    }
    while(c<4);
}
void draw(double edge[20][3])
{
    initgraph(&gd,&gm,(char *)"");
    line(320,240,320,25);
    line(320,240,550,240);
    line(320,240,150,410);
    for(int i=0; i<19; i++)
    {
        x1=edge[i][0]+edge[i][2]*(cos(2.3562));
        y3=(double)(edge[i][1]-edge[i][2]*(sin(2.3562)));
        x2=edge[i+1][0]+edge[i+1][2]*(cos(2.3562));
        y2=edge[i+1][1]-edge[i+1][2]*(sin(2.3562));
        line(x1+320,240-y3,x2+320,240-y2);
    }
    getch();
    closegraph();
}

05/03/23, 9:58â€¯am - Kanishk Pratap Singh: #include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

int binarySearch(int arr[],int low, int high, int item){
    while((high-low) >1){
        int mid=(low+high)/2;
        if(arr[mid]==item)
            return mid;
        if(arr[mid]<item)
            low=mid+1;
        else
            high=mid-1;
    }
    return -1;
}


int main(void){
    int n,item;
    cout<<"enter number of elements in array"<<endl;
    cin>>n;
    int arr[n];
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
        cin>>arr[i];
    }
    cout<<"element to be found"<<endl;
    cin>>item;
    int result = binarySearch(arr,0,n-1,item);
    return result;
}
